By manually breaking these cycles, Python's reference counting can immediately reclaim memory without waiting for garbage collection.\n\n## Root Cause\nTwo reference cycles prevent garbage collection:\n1. **Graph cycle**: `Graph -> nodes (doubly linked list) -> graph`\n2. **FakeTensorMode cycle**: `FakeTensorMode -> ShapeEnv -> TrackedFake -> FakeTensor -> FakeTensorMode`\n\nThese cycles cause memory to be held until full GC, which can take ~150ms per failed graph.\n\n## Solution\nManually break the reference cycles by:\n1. Clearing graph node metadata and unlinking nodes from the graph's doubly-linked-list\n2. Setting ShapeEnv.tracked_fakes to None\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### File 1: torch/_dynamo/output_graph.py\n**Method**: `cleanup()` (line ~2228)\n\n**Changes**:\n- After line 2247 (`self.backward_state.clear()`), add:\n  - By manually breaking these cycles, Python's reference counting can immediately reclaim memory without waiting for garbage collection.\n\n## Root Cause\nTwo reference cycles prevent garbage collection:\n1. **Graph cycle**: `Graph -> nodes (doubly linked list) -> graph`\n2. **FakeTensorMode cycle**: `FakeTensorMode -> ShapeEnv -> TrackedFake -> FakeTensor -> FakeTensorMode`\n\nThese cycles cause memory to be held until full GC, which can take ~150ms per failed graph.\n\n## Solution\nManually break the reference cycles by:\n1. Clearing graph node metadata and unlinking nodes from the doubly-linked list\n2. Setting ShapeEnv.tracked_fakes to None\n\n## Files to Modify (2 main files)\n\n### File 1: torch/_dynamo/output_graph.py\n**Location**: `cleanup()` method (around line 2228)\n**Change**: Add 19 lines after `self.backward_state.clear()`\n\n**What to add**:\n```python\n# Cleanup graph nodes to break reference cycles.\nfor node in list(self.graph.nodes):\n    node.meta.clear()\n    node._remove_from_list()\n\n# Cleanup ShapeEnv's tracked_fakes to break reference cycle\nif self.tracing_context.fake_mode is not None:\n    shape_env = self.tracing_context.fake_mode.shape_env\n    if shape_env is not None:\n        shape_env.tracked_fakes = None\n```\n\n### File 2: torch/_dynamo/convert_frame.py\n**Location**: finally block (around line 1280)\n**Change**: Add 5 lines after `tracer.f_locals = {}`\n\n**What to add**:\n```python\n# Cleanup failed tracer outputs to break reference cycles\nif tracer.output and fail_reason is not None:\n    tracer.output.cleanup()\n```\n\n## Key Implementation Details\n\n✓ **Thread-safe**: Uses conditional checks to prevent errors\n✓ **Non-disruptive**: Only affects failed compilations (fail_reason != None)\n✓ **No API changes**: Pure cleanup improvement\n✓ **Backward compatible**: No changes to public interfaces\n\n## Documentation Provided\n\nIn `/workspace/`, you'll find:\n\n1. **IMPLEMENTATION_GUIDE.txt** -
